< Text>
Excellent co-op style shop for music lovers! The staff are knowledgeable and friendly. The products are all top notch and made in America (if not made a few miles from there). They seem to value and support the local musicians and craftsmen more than any other place I have been. They have a small selection of used and signed records that are surprisingly high quality and include many rare albums. They also have a selection of extremely nice strats and telecasters, some with an intential worn patina that suits them well. Aside from the products, they also offer live music from local musicians quite often. The support they show for local musicians and the community is heartwarming. I strongly recommend stopping buy.</Text>

<date>1566772797929<//date>< Review>
Fallbrook youth baseball field and Ingold sports park is always confusing, and it is hard to find.  You have to search for Ingold sports park. They both are same, unfortunately  but little apart with in a big field and not walkable.

This is a large sports complex with small parking spots. No restrooms available but found a porta potty.

Great for kids and for the spectators.  Beautiful drive tho this field,  make sure you know where you are going before you leave,  tricky to find thia spot.

4 fields, nicely maintained with dirt and real grass.

Good luck finding it.< /Review>

<rating>5<//rating><Gmap_id>0x80dd2d73bb8af4cf:0x676cab11b57db5be< /Gmap_id><user_id>101501762218714979803< /user_id><resp>None< /resp><pictures>None</pictures>< review>
Great place for ice cream treats. I love DQ and this one is overall great. My favorite thing is the Blizzard and I enjoy trying new flavors/combinations. The staff here is friendly and efficient. The parking can be tough on weekend nights due to neighboring club/restaurant so be prepared to wait a few minutes or drive around the lot a bit to find parking. If there's one complaint I have about this DQ it's that their medium size blizzard is never fully mixed. There is always about an inch or so of the soft serve vanilla at the bottom. It seems like by now DQ should have perfected the Blizzard making process so that it would all be mixed equally, but after many visits, it's always that way. After you eat a bit, you have to try to mix it yourself with the flimsy plastic spoon. Doesn't stop me from coming back though. This is a great DQ with a great staff!</review>

<Date>1540275743733</Date><user_name>Lady Snow< /user_name></record></dataset><record>
<user_id>102918253898437847981</user_id>< gmap_id>
0x80dd2d73bb8af4cf:0x676cab11b57db5be<//gmap_id>
<Date>1416255997488< /Date><user_name>Rodney S<//user_name><rating>3< /rating><Response>None<//Response>< Text>
The Lacto-King visits the Dairy Queen for some Orange Julius.

BOGO coupon for Original Orange Julius or Smoothies.

Back in the day, I remember Los Cerritos Center had an Orange Julius.  This was when the mall had a Time Out arcade, a trashy UA Twin theater, a Woolworth and a piano/organ store.  I was uber cool, with my Stussy apparel, sunglasses with straps and velcro Pro Wings.  Can't forget the Sun-In in my wavy locks, either ;p  In all my years walking up and down the mall, I never had an Orange Julius.  Was I missing something?  Was my life incomplete?

Opening up my inbox and finding a BOGO coupon,  I found another bucketlist moment - Try an Orange Julius.

Dairy Queen is across the street from Los Cerritos Center.  Besides the usual DQ faves such as Blizzards, hamburgers and dogs,  DQ also sells Orange Julius products.

I ordered 2 large original Orange Julius'.  I asked the employee if it's like Orange Bang.  He didn't know what Orange Bang was (really?), so I slipped on my food critic hat and had my first sips of this frozen, sugary concoction-
Orange Icee is what came to mind.  The texture was smooth, it wasn't overly sweet and was quite refreshing on this warm day.  Like Orange Bang?  No, unfortunately.  Orange Bang is whipped, frothy and just that much more better.  The price was good, though.  Using my BOGO coupon, the damage including tax was $3.80.  Not too shabby, frugal one!

Service was good, as I chatted fruit trees and Indian food with the employee.  I owe him a Chico tree seedling ;p

The place was clean with tables for seating.  The blenders are going non-stop, so not a place to catch up with a friend or get some studying done.  The parking lot is a little on the small side.

Of course, the ice cream is what people go to DQ for.  I'll be back, moreso for a Blizzard or ice cream  than another Orange Julius.

Recommend!

NOMNOMNOMNONNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOM</Text>
